name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Family-friendly Family Room
info:Stayed in February 2024

rating:3.5
posted:Posted February 20, 2024
msg:The hotel is very big. The advantage of an old hotel is that the rooms are large, but the disadvantage is that the decoration is old.
The bedding and room hygiene were done well, and a welcome fruit plate and drinks were given.
The response speed of room service is fast and the attitude is relatively good.
The bathroom showerhead was severely clogged.
It takes ten or twenty minutes to walk from the hotel to the Mizoguchi ticket check-in area. Turn right when you exit the hotel and you will find the passenger terminal, but there are only long-distance buses.
There is only one small restaurant and a small supermarket within a 10-minute walk around the hotel. It is very deserted and all kinds of shops are vacant, making it inconvenient to travel for food and drinks.
After staying for 3 days, the hotel's hot spring was not turned on, and the hot water was not stable at night. On the morning of check-out, even the air conditioner could not blow hot air.
The hotel lobby and restaurant are very dark, and the massage chair area is the only bright place.
The breakfast at the hotel was terrible. I only ate it once and never went to that restaurant again. There is only one waiter who clears the tableware, and his communication attitude is very poor. Only the fruits for breakfast are fresh, and corn and sweet potatoes are dry and inferior products with black marks.

The check-in is fast at the front desk. It is open for steaming and steaming. It is very convenient to have a changing room in the hot spring area. The hot spring is very comfortable. The parent-child room is large, clean and tidy. The sofa is very clean. The bed is dry and comfortable. Free mineral water, tea bags, safe in the room, clean and no scale in the kettle, breakfast buffet with Chinese and Western style, rich variety, dinner in the hotel, the meals are full, delicious, reasonable price, beautiful environment, both breakfast and dinner time The staff carried the teapot and delivered butter tea from table to table. msg:The location of the hotel is excellent. It is near the Jiuzhaigou scenic spot. It takes three minutes by taxi, ten minutes on foot, and usually you can walk to the entrance of the scenic spot in fifteen minutes. The rooms are clean and tidy, and there are many types of breakfast in the hotel. Especially the hotel service is first-rate, free of charge from the airport to the hotel. The front desk service made me very satisfied. Due to the weather, our Air China flight from Chengdu to Jiuzhaigou on September 25 was cancelled, which caused the room we booked on the 25th to be unavailable. I called the hotel front desk to negotiate with Ctrip and finally waived it. I paid for the day. I am very touched by such an honest hotel. I will definitely stay at this hotel next time I come to Jiuzhaigou. I will recommend my relatives and friends to Jiuzhaigou!
